\subsection*{Additional Inherited Members}


\subsection{Detailed Description}
Radiotap header implementation. 

Radiotap is a de facto standard for 802.\+11 frame injection and reception. The radiotap header format is a mechanism to supply additional information about frames, from the driver to userspace applications such as libpcap, and from a userspace application to the driver for transmission.

\subsection{Member Function Documentation}
\index{ns3\+::\+Radiotap\+Header@{ns3\+::\+Radiotap\+Header}!Deserialize@{Deserialize}}
\index{Deserialize@{Deserialize}!ns3\+::\+Radiotap\+Header@{ns3\+::\+Radiotap\+Header}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{Deserialize(\+Buffer\+::\+Iterator start)}{Deserialize(Buffer::Iterator start)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}uint32\+\_\+t ns3\+::\+Radiotap\+Header\+::\+Deserialize (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf Buffer\+::\+Iterator}}]{start}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}\hypertarget{classns3_1_1RadiotapHeader_abf6c96491c49ece598cc16737b0696a7}{}\label{classns3_1_1RadiotapHeader_abf6c96491c49ece598cc16737b0696a7}
This method is used by \hyperlink{classns3_1_1Packet_a0961eccf975d75f902d40956c93ba63e}{Packet\+::\+Remove\+Header} to re-\/create a header from the byte buffer of a packet. The data read is expected to match bit-\/for-\/bit the representation of this header in real networks.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em start} & An iterator which points to where the header should written. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The number of bytes read. 
\end{DoxyReturn}


Implements \hyperlink{classns3_1_1Header_a78be9400bb66b2a8543606f395ef5396}{ns3\+::\+Header}.

446       \hyperlink{classns3_1_1RadiotapHeader_a229fb0939d24f5f2ea73c31c228b0fb1}{m\_ampduStatusPad} = ((4 - bytesRead % 4) % 4);
447       \hyperlink{namespacevisualizer_1_1core_a2a35e5d8a34af358b508dac8635754e0}{start}.Next (\hyperlink{classns3_1_1RadiotapHeader_a229fb0939d24f5f2ea73c31c228b0fb1}{m\_ampduStatusPad});
448       \hyperlink{classns3_1_1RadiotapHeader_a8be72c0459a3f52b873bb3cc8899885c}{m\_ampduStatusRef} = \hyperlink{namespacevisualizer_1_1core_a2a35e5d8a34af358b508dac8635754e0}{start}.ReadU32 ();
449       \hyperlink{classns3_1_1RadiotapHeader_a17349b310a739e281683073ee042ceab}{m\_ampduStatusFlags} = \hyperlink{namespacevisualizer_1_1core_a2a35e5d8a34af358b508dac8635754e0}{start}.ReadU16 ();
450       \hyperlink{classns3_1_1RadiotapHeader_a05ed1ce716402a0c1609a3203d4fbccb}{m\_ampduStatusCRC} = \hyperlink{namespacevisualizer_1_1core_a2a35e5d8a34af358b508dac8635754e0}{start}.ReadU8 ();
451       \hyperlink{namespacevisualizer_1_1core_a2a35e5d8a34af358b508dac8635754e0}{start}.ReadU8 ();
452       bytesRead += (8 + \hyperlink{classns3_1_1RadiotapHeader_a229fb0939d24f5f2ea73c31c228b0fb1}{m\_ampduStatusPad});
453     \}
454 
455   \textcolor{comment}{//}
456   \textcolor{comment}{// Information about the received or transmitted VHT frame.}
457   \textcolor{comment}{//}
458   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (\hyperlink{classns3_1_1RadiotapHeader_a8b8aca212245ad4ad1aa796d4cc802bb}{m\_present} & \hyperlink{classns3_1_1RadiotapHeader_afd15dfe66387dfbcbf62865d024f58ffa42c8ef18aeb45f077a5e1d7c436a134a}{RADIOTAP\_VHT}) \textcolor{comment}{// bit 21}
459     \{
460       \hyperlink{classns3_1_1RadiotapHeader_ae9875044826afec2aefbaaa79672faa7}{m\_vhtPad} = ((2 - bytesRead % 2) % 2);
461       \hyperlink{namespacevisualizer_1_1core_a2a35e5d8a34af358b508dac8635754e0}{start}.Next (\hyperlink{classns3_1_1RadiotapHeader_ae9875044826afec2aefbaaa79672faa7}{m\_vhtPad});
462       \hyperlink{classns3_1_1RadiotapHeader_ae0560a9f80ce1e8693a88ba3a233e09d}{m\_vhtKnown} = \hyperlink{namespacevisualizer_1_1core_a2a35e5d8a34af358b508dac8635754e0}{start}.ReadU16 ();
463       \hyperlink{classns3_1_1RadiotapHeader_ae1f2319399552e40d53d888516bf7445}{m\_vhtFlags} = \hyperlink{namespacevisualizer_1_1core_a2a35e5d8a34af358b508dac8635754e0}{start}.ReadU8 ();
464       \hyperlink{classns3_1_1RadiotapHeader_a5a21360554e80b96114f79c2e315fffe}{m\_vhtBandwidth} = \hyperlink{namespacevisualizer_1_1core_a2a35e5d8a34af358b508dac8635754e0}{start}.ReadU8 ();
465       \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (uint8\_t \hyperlink{bernuolliDistribution_8m_a6f6ccfcf58b31cb6412107d9d5281426}{i} = 0; \hyperlink{bernuolliDistribution_8m_a6f6ccfcf58b31cb6412107d9d5281426}{i} < 4; \hyperlink{bernuolliDistribution_8m_a6f6ccfcf58b31cb6412107d9d5281426}{i}++)
466         \{
467           \hyperlink{classns3_1_1RadiotapHeader_a771386b3e7e6bbc2e44a241ae6cf1797}{m\_vhtMcsNss}[\hyperlink{bernuolliDistribution_8m_a6f6ccfcf58b31cb6412107d9d5281426}{i}] = \hyperlink{namespacevisualizer_1_1core_a2a35e5d8a34af358b508dac8635754e0}{start}.ReadU8 ();
468         \}
469       \hyperlink{classns3_1_1RadiotapHeader_a6d4b9a2225cf4343df89a95097baa603}{m\_vhtCoding} = \hyperlink{namespacevisualizer_1_1core_a2a35e5d8a34af358b508dac8635754e0}{start}.ReadU8 ();
470       \hyperlink{classns3_1_1RadiotapHeader_a17096a7c0cea398b1a80a1789b6fcd6f}{m\_vhtGroupId} = \hyperlink{namespacevisualizer_1_1core_a2a35e5d8a34af358b508dac8635754e0}{start}.ReadU8 ();
471       \hyperlink{classns3_1_1RadiotapHeader_a39d6fde2fceecb55e847f28e89f2ed4d}{m\_vhtPartialAid} = \hyperlink{namespacevisualizer_1_1core_a2a35e5d8a34af358b508dac8635754e0}{start}.ReadU16 ();
472       bytesRead += (12 + \hyperlink{classns3_1_1RadiotapHeader_ae9875044826afec2aefbaaa79672faa7}{m\_vhtPad});
473     \}
474 
475   \hyperlink{assert_8h_aff5ece9066c74e681e74999856f08539}{NS\_ASSERT\_MSG} (\hyperlink{classns3_1_1RadiotapHeader_a6894ef017e95e58463eac5e435507a33}{m\_length} == bytesRead, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"RadiotapHeader::Deserialize(): expected and
       actual lengths inconsistent"});
476   \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} bytesRead;
477 \}
\end{DoxyCode}

\index{ns3\+::\+Radiotap\+Header@{ns3\+::\+Radiotap\+Header}!Get\+Serialized\+Size@{Get\+Serialized\+Size}}

\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{Get\+Serialized\+Size(void) const }{GetSerializedSize(void) const }}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}uint32\+\_\+t ns3\+::\+Radiotap\+Header\+::\+Get\+Serialized\+Size (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}

This method is used by \hyperlink{classns3_1_1Packet_a465108c595a0bc592095cbcab1832ed8}{Packet\+::\+Add\+Header} to store the header into the byte buffer of a packet. This method returns the number of bytes which are needed to store the header data during a Serialize.

\index{ns3\+::\+Radiotap\+Header@{ns3\+::\+Radiotap\+Header}!Print@{Print}}
\index{Print@{Print}!ns3\+::\+Radiotap\+Header@{ns3\+::\+Radiotap\+Header}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{Print(std\+::ostream \&os) const }{Print(std::ostream &os) const }}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void ns3\+::\+Radiotap\+Header\+::\+Print (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{std\+::ostream \&}]{os}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}\hypertarget{classns3_1_1RadiotapHeader_aba8a0323732b5d6d48dd2cc50b7ed9fe}{}\label{classns3_1_1RadiotapHeader_aba8a0323732b5d6d48dd2cc50b7ed9fe}
This method is used by \hyperlink{classns3_1_1Packet_aa34058a5cdbf94673531f8c4001ab227}{Packet\+::\+Print} to print the content of the header as ascii data to a C++ output stream. Although the header is free to format its output as it wishes, it is recommended to follow a few rules to integrate with the packet pretty printer\+: start with flags, small field values located between a pair of parens. Values should be separated by whitespace. Follow the parens with the important fields, separated by whitespace.

eg\+: (field1 val1 field2 val2 field3 val3) field4 val4 field5 val5


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em os} & The output stream \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}


Implements \hyperlink{classns3_1_1Header_a2ce1df7579b2ade7bc7302357feac77a}{ns3\+::\+Header}.

\index{ns3\+::\+Radiotap\+Header@{ns3\+::\+Radiotap\+Header}!Serialize@{Serialize}}
\index{Serialize@{Serialize}!ns3\+::\+Radiotap\+Header@{ns3\+::\+Radiotap\+Header}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{Serialize(\+Buffer\+::\+Iterator start) const }{Serialize(Buffer::Iterator start) const }}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void ns3\+::\+Radiotap\+Header\+::\+Serialize (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf Buffer\+::\+Iterator}}]{start}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}\hypertarget{classns3_1_1RadiotapHeader_a31d78b190e1969d9216e3be630b2b129}{}\label{classns3_1_1RadiotapHeader_a31d78b190e1969d9216e3be630b2b129}
This method is used by \hyperlink{classns3_1_1Packet_a465108c595a0bc592095cbcab1832ed8}{Packet\+::\+Add\+Header} to store the header into the byte buffer of a packet. The data written is expected to match bit-\/for-\/bit the representation of this header in a real network.
